1b1(rgyud): rgya gar skad du/ Ar+ya pany+tsa bang sha ti pradz+nyApUr mr-i
1b2(rgyud): ma ma hA yAn sU tra/ bod skad du/ 'phags
1b3(rgyud): date nanade
1b4(rgyud): shurtsa lnga pa zhes bya ba theg pa chen po'i mdo/ sangs rgyas
1b5(rgyud): tra/ dro/ ri ru 'e tA'e Sh+ra/ tra/ dra/ kra kra shrekra/ tra/ rA R+sha tr-i/ kr-i ra/ tro/ dra/ ShAda?/ nga?/
2a1(rgyud): #/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad
2a2(rgyud): bdag gis thos pa du se gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das ri rab kyi zoms la lha thams
2a3(rgyud): cad kyi mtshan mo'i gnas na/ byang chub sems dpa' bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag du
2a4(rgyud): ma dang thabs cig tu bzhugs te/ de nas bcom ldan 'das lha dang /
2b1(rgyud): lha ma yin dang / rlung lha dang / nam mkha' lding dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / mi 'am ci dang / srin po dang / rig
2b2(rgyud): sngags 'chang tha mas cad dang / 'byung po dang / log 'dren dang / sha za dang / snang ba dang / mi snang ba'i ma mo'i tshogs
2b3(rgyud): shin tu mang zhing rgya che ba dpag tshad lnga'i dkyil 'khor du 'dus pa sha stag dang / dge slong stong nyis brgya lnga bcus bskor
2b4(rgyud): cing mdun du bdar nas chos ston te/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po lag na rdo rje/ rdo rje'i rigs
2b5(rgyud): thams cad kyis yongs su bskor cing rig pa'i tshogs dang / phyag rgya'i tshogs de dag thams cad kyi rig sngags 'chang bye
3a1(rgyud): #/ ba phrag du mas yongs su bskor nas/ bcom ldan 'das ga la ba der song ste phyin nas bar snang las babs
3a2(rgyud): nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal te/ bcom ldan 'das la lan gsum bskor ba byas nas phyogs gcig
3a3(rgyud): tu 'dug pa dang / de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis/ gsang ba'i bdag po lag na rdo rje la bka' stsal pa/ gsang ba'i bdag po nyi shu
3a4(rgyud): rtsa lnga po 'di rnams ni/ nga'i shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo yin no// oM sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad
3a5(rgyud): la phyag 'tshal lo// oM byang chub kyi sems rdo rje shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM kun tu bzang po spyod pa shes rab kyi
3a6(rgyud): pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// i yid bzhin gyi nor bu shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM 'gog pa med pa shes rab kyi pha rol
3b1(rgyud): tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM skye bar 'gyur ba shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM rnam par shes pa thams cad shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM 'bar ba chen po'i chos nyid/
3b2(rgyud): shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM brtson 'grus shes rab kyi pha rol tu byin pa'i sgo'o// oM thams cad du 'gro ba shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgro'o// oM rdo rje thams
3b3(rgyud): cad brtan pa'i sems shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM rang bzhin rnam par dag pa'i
3b4(rgyud): chos nyid ye shes rnam par dag pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM las rnam par skyong ba shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM nges par gnod mdzes rdo rje can/
3b5(rgyud): phaT shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM 'dod pa la 'dod chags rnam par dag pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM mgyogs pa'i rdo rje can shes rab kyi pha
3b6(rgyud): rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM hUM thams cad du 'gro ba shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// sro gyi shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgra'o// au a zhes bya ba'i sgo shes rab
3b7(rgyud): kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM aM ba hUM shaus rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM aM shes
4a1(rgyud): rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku'i mchog shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM de bzhin gshegs pa
4a2(rgyud): thams cad kyi gsung rnam par dag pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs kyi rdo rje shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o//
4a3(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das kyis de skad ces bka' stsal nas/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po lag na rdo rje dang / thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor de dag dang / lha dang /
4a4(rgyud): mi dang / lha ma yin dang / dri zar bcas pa'i 'jig rten yi rangs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa la mngon par bstod de// 'phags pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin
4a5(rgyud): pa'i sgo nyi shu rtsa lnga pa zhes bya ba theg pa chen po'i mdo rdzogs so// rgya gar skad du/ sarba ta thA ga ta kA ya bA k+Shit+ta gu h+ya a
4a6(rgyud): lang+ga ra bru ho tan+t+ra rA dzA nA ma/ bod skad du/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi gsang ba rgyan gyi bkod pa zhes bya ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po
4a7(rgyud): bla ma dang 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi zhabs kyi pad+mo la gus par phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa zam
4b1(rgyud): cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje ye shes rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdorje
4b2(rgyud): ye shes phyag rgya chen po'i dam tshig gi byin gyi rlabs kyi rdo rje'i sku chen po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje ye shes rin po che chen
4b3(rgyud): po'i cod pan gyi rtse mo'i gtsug bud kyis dbang bskur ba brnyes pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje ye shes kyi ting nge 'dzin chen
4b4(rgyud): po dang ldan pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje ye shes kyi las sna tshogs pa chen po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa tham
4b5(rgyud): cad kyi sku dang gsung dang / thugs rdo rje ye shes mchod pa chen po spo ba'i dam tshig gi gsang ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang /
4b6(rgyud): thugs rdo rje ye shes dkyil 'khor chen po dam tshig gi de kho na nyid dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje ye shes gsang
4b7(rgyud): ba chen po'i snying po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje ye shes kyi mnga' bdag chen po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams/
5a1(rgyud): cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje ye shes kun tu bzang po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje
5a2(rgyud): ye shes dpe med cing mi mnyam pa dang mnyam pa nam mkha' lta bu dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje rigs dang / snying po dang /
5a3(rgyud): phyag rgya dang / gsang sngags dang / rig pa gnyis su med par gyur pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje ye shes pha rol tu phyin
5a4(rgyud): pa'i snying po la dga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje ye shes kyi lhag pa'i lha'i snying po mdzes pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa
5a5(rgyud): thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje ye shes rgyan chen po bkod pa'i dkyil 'khor chen po'i snying po la/ nam mkha'i khams thams cad kyi rdul phra rab kyi rdul dang
5a6(rgyud): mnyam pa'i rdo rje ye shes chen po 'ba' zhig dang thabs cig tu bzhugs so// de'ang 'di lta ste/ sgo mtha' yas pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje yum chen mo dang / nam mkha'i sgo zhes bya
5a7(rgyud): ba'i rdo rje yum chen mo dang / a po dza'i sgo zhes bya ba'i rdo rje yum chen mo dang / 'gyur ba med pa'i sgo zhes bya ba'i rdo rje yum chen mo dang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin ma zhes bya
5b1(rgyud): ba'i rdo rje yum chen mo dang / gzhan yang ma lus shing lus pa med pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul phra rab dang mnyam pa'i brtson 'grus dang ldan pa'i rdo rje btsun mo stong phrag
5b2(rgyud): brgya lnga'ang 'di lta ste/ madra'i mchod tshwa'i lag ces bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / dbang phyug lA lta ba'i rim pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / nye bar zhi ba'i bzhin ras zhes
5b3(rgyud): bya ba'i rdo rje btsun ma dang / gyen du lta bu'i bzhin ras zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / 'dod pa'i zla mtshan rdo rje zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / brda sprod pa ma zhes bya ba'i rdo rje
5b4(rgyud): btsun mo dang / 'bri ba'i sgo zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / rol pa dang ldan pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / 'dod pa'i mchog ces bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / dbang phyug gis
5b5(rgyud): bde ba'i sgo zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / dmigs pa'i sgo zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / brang las skyes zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo ste/ de dag la sogs pa rdo rje btsun mo rnam
5b6(rgyud): kyis yongs su bskor cing mdun du bdar to// gzhan yang dpag tu med pa'i rdo rje pho nya mo chen mo rnams dang thabs cig tu bzhugs te/ de'ang 'di lta ste/ snying skul bar byed pa zhes
5b7(rgyud): bya ba'i rdo rje pho nya mo chen mo dang / gdug pa thams cad 'gugs pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje po nya mo chen mo dang / rjes su mnyes pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i rdo rje pho nya mo chen mo dang / khrag 'gugs
6a1(rgyud): pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje pho nya mo chen mo dang / thams cad 'phrog pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje pho nya mo chen mo la sogs pa'o// gzhan yang 'jig rten gyi khams rgyas
6a2(rgyud): pa'i rdo rje sgo srungs ma chen mo rnams dang yang thabs cig ste/ de'ang 'di lta ste/ rdo rje 'bebs pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje sgo srungs ma chen mo dang / dam tshig gsum ldan zhes bya ba'i rdo rje
6a3(rgyud): sgo srungs ma chen mo dang / 'jig pa'i yan lag can zhes bya ba'i rdo rje sgo srungs ma chen mo dang / thog ma pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje sgo srungs ma chen mo dang / gdul dka' 'dul zhes bya
6a4(rgyud): ba'i rdo rje sgo srungs ma chen mo la sogs pa'o// gzhan yang mi mnyam pa dang mnyam pa'i rdo rje bran mo chen mo rnams dang yang thabs cig ste/ de'ang 'di lta ste/ sku gsung thugs
6a5(rgyud): thams cad rdo rjes 'ching ba ma zhes bya ba'i rdo rje bran mo chen mo dang / 'jigs pa'i me'i gdong zhes bya ba'i rdo rje bran mo chen mo dang / gtsigs shing rnam par 'gyur ba'i gdong
6a6(rgyud): zhes bya ba'i rdo rje bran mo chen dang / 'jig rten gsum 'ching ba zhes bya ba'i rdo rje bran mo chen mo dang / bskul par gnas pa zhes bya ba la sogs pa'i rdo rje bran mo chen mo'o//
6a7(rgyud): gzhan yang dpe med pa'i rdo rje rol pa mo chen mo rnams dang yang thabs cig ste/ de'ang 'di lta ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku gsung thugs rdo rje dgyes pa zhes
6b1(rgyud): bya ba'i rdo rje rol pa chen mo dang / kun nas 'bebs pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje rol pa chen mo dang / 'jig rten gsum rab tu 'joms pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje rol pa chen mo dang / rab tu dag
6b2(rgyud): ba'i rjes su 'gro ba zhes bya ba'i rdo rje rol pa chen mo dang / thams cad dga' bar byed pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje rol pa chen mo la sogs pa'o// gzhan yang dam mkha'i khams thams cad
6b3(rgyud): rgyas par gang ba'i rdo rje'i yab rnams dang yang thabs cig ste/ de'ang 'di lta ste/ 'dod pa'i dbang phyug ces bya ba'i rdo rje yab chen po dang / mkha' 'gro'i rdo rje dbang phyug dang /
6b4(rgyud): dri yi dbang phyug dang / stug po bkod pa dang / zla ba'i 'od dang / 'dun pa bsrel dang / skye bo yongs su dor ba dang / legs par sbyangs pa dang / 'dod pa'i rdo rje dang // gdung
6b5(rgyud): bskyed pa dang / 'dul bar byed pa dang / gdug pa thams cad sel bar byed pa dang / de kho na nyid kyi mgon po dang / gnas pa po dang / brtse ba can dang / chos 'chang dang
6b6(rgyud): bskyod pa po dang / spo ba po dang / 'ching ba po dang / skor ba po dang / de dag la sogs pa rdo rje yab rnams so// gzhan yang mtha' yas pa'i rdo rje po nya mo 'phrog pa'i rdo rje bran pa
6b7(rgyud): rdo rje'i tshogs dang thabs cig ste/ de'ang 'di lta ste/ rdo rje rlung zhes bya ba dang / rdo rje me dang / rdo rje mi 'khrugs pa dang / rdo rje chu dang / gzhan yang rdo rje rgyal po chen po bzhi la/
7a1(rgyud): 'di lta ste/ zhi bar byed pa dang / rgyas par byed pa dang / dbang du byed pa dang / mi shes pa thams cad zad par byed pa ste/ de dag la sogs pa'o//
7a2(rgyud): gzhan yang mchog tu rgya chen po sangs rgyas kyi ye shes rab tu gnas pa'i mchod pa dang ldan pa bcom ldan 'das ston pa rtag pa mchog gi mnga' bdag ste/ kun tu bzang po'i sku yis
7a3(rgyud): ni/ 'jig rten gsum gyi dkyil 'khor spros// bcom ldan rdo rje 'dzin legs bzhugs// gsang ba rgyan gyi sbyor bas so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad skyed par
7a4(rgyud): byed pa'i yum gsang ba'i rdo rje 'dus pa thob ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yab dang lhan cig tu dga' ba'i bde ba rjes su byung ste 'khor dang bcas pa rnams bcom
7a5(rgyud): ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar lhags te/ rdo rje'i glu 'dis mngon par bstod nas zhu ba zhus pa/ sangs rgyas kun don khyod phyag 'tshal// rdo rje 'byung ba khyod la 'dud// thugs kyi
7a6(rgyud): rin chen mchog khyod 'dud// chos kyi blo gros khyod la 'dud// chos rnams kun mchog khyod la 'dud// sna tshogs dgongs pa khyod la 'dud// dam tshigs mchog gi mchog khyod 'dud// rdo rje sems dpa'
7a7(rgyud): phyag 'tshal 'dud// grags pa chen po bdag cag ni// mgon po khyod la zhu ba zhu// sangs rgyas thams cad skyed byed yum// dkyil 'khor gyi ni dkyil 'khor mchog/ de nas/
7b1(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das rdo rje sems dpa' des de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje'i yum rnams la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yum rnams de skad pa
7b2(rgyud): smra zhig/ 'jig rten thams cad la khyab pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi rgyal po chen po 'di la ma 'ongs pa'i sems can rnams dad par mi 'gyur zhing / rang gi sems yongs su sun 'byir la/
7b3(rgyud): des ma mthong ba'i chos la ma dad pas rang gi sems yang dag par sun phyung ste/ mnar med pa rnams su skyes nas bskal pa stong phrag mang por mnar med pa'i sdug bsngal rjes su 'byung bar
7b4(rgyud): 'gyur ro// de brgya lam na mnar med pa'i sdug bsngal las grol te/ mi rnams su skyes par gyur kyang rnam par 'gyur ba bzhin du 'gyur ro// brjed ngas pa rnams dang / blo gros chung
7b5(rgyud): ba rnams dang / khyi dang / bya rog dang / byi la dang / bag dang / stag dang / glang po che dang / seng ge'i nga ro 'dra ba dag tu 'gyur ro// de dang 'gro bar mi bya zhing blta bar mi bya'o//
7b6(rgyud): de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad bskyed pa'i yum de rnams kyis/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das ji ltar sems can de rnams kyi mnar med
7b7(rgyud): pa'i sdug bsngal zad par 'gyur/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ gang gis 'di'i ming bzung nas yongs su zad par 'gyur ro// bsod nams de'i rgyus de'i las
8a1(rgyud): kyi sgrib pa zad pa de bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi skul btsun du 'gyur ro// de nas de dag yid dga' ba skyes nas yang / bcom ldan 'das
8a2(rgyud): la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bstan du gsol/ bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs kyi rgyus dkyil 'khor chen po'i rgyal po sems can thams cad la phan pa dang
8a3(rgyud): bde ba'i phyir/ gang ma 'ongs pa'i sems can rnams kyis dran pa tsam gyis sangs rgyas kyi byang chub thob par 'gyur ro// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis kun tu bzang po chen po 'ad
8a4(rgyud): 'phro ba gsal ba rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so// rang gi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje rnams las de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku'i dam/
8a5(rgyud): pa 'di bka' stsal pa/ dkyil 'khor kun gyi yum gyur pa// stong nyid ye shes nyid du bshad// ci zhig nga yis bstan par bya// rtog pa thams cad rnam par spangs// sems
8a6(rgyud): can rnams la phan bzhed pa// gang zhig cung zad bstan par bya// de kun sgyu mas sgyu ma'o// 'gro ba sgyu ma lta bur shes// des na sgyu ma lta bu yis// sgyu ma lta bu'i dkyil 'khor bya/
8a7(rgyud): nam mkha'i khams kyis khyab pa yis// thams cad yum gyis yang dge 'khrugs// phyi rol yang ni brtag par bya// gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor yum rnams kyis// dben zhing
8b1(rgyud): dga' ba'i gnas su ni// yid kyis legs par 'dus byas pa// nam mkha' la ni thig gis gdab// thog mar de yis dam pas so// de nas rnal 'byor chen pos thig/ gsang ba'i/
8b2(rgyud): yum gyi dkyil 'khor ro// pu khyud dag gi rnam bdun du// kun nas yongs su bskor bar bya// dbus kyi cha ru dkyil 'khor ni// 'khor lo lta bur bri bar bya// kun+da nas brgyad gnyis
8b3(rgyud): mdzes pa ni// dkyil 'khor bzhi yi dbus su'o// 'khor lo'i lte ba'i dbus su ni// pad+ma ze 'bru ldan pa bri// mtshams dang mtshams su 'drab ma ni// ji lta ba bzhin bsnyems
8b4(rgyud): bcas pas// srad bu lnga yis yang dag 'khrugs// srad bu bzhi yis nye bar sbas// sgo bzhi dang ni yang dag ldan// rta babs seng ge dag gis brgyan// gdugs dang rgyal mtshan
8b5(rgyud): ba dan sogs// bla res steng du bres pa dang // rin chen rdo rje pad ldan sngon// dpag bsam shing gi lcug mas khyab// bum bzang rin chen ldan pa'i mchog/ rgyan 'breng glang po ldan pa
8b6(rgyud): ni// phyi rol gnas te legs par bri// rtog dang mi rtog rnam spangs te// dkyil 'khor chen po'i dbus su ni// gsang ba rgyan gyi rdo rje bya// mnyam par gzhag cing spro ba yis// sem
8b7(rgyud): kyis bri ba nyid du bya// de nas lha mo zhal bzhi ma// shes rab pha rol phyin dge ba// phyag bzhi pa la spyan yangs ma// phyag gnyis kyis ni chos 'chad cing // zhi ba'i g.yas par
9a1(rgyud): rdo rje ste// g.yon pa bad+mas rnam par brgyad// dkar dang dmar po cher rdzob// sngo bsangs rin chen mchog mdzes 'od// gtsug na rin chen gtsug tor che/
9a2(rgyud): gtsug rgyan cod pan dam pa can// skal ba chen po 'od ldan ma// rgyan rnams kun gyis rnam par klubs// gos kyis lto ni legs bsgribs pa// bzhin gyi dkyil 'khor 'dzub bcas shing /
9a3(rgyud): sna tshogs gos ni legs gyon pa// dbu ma'i zhal ras gser gyi 'od// zhabs gnyis dbus su 'khor lo lte// mdun na rin chen bdun gnas pa// pad+ma mchog ldan seng ge'i khri/
9a4(rgyud): zla ba rdo rje 'dzin pa'i gdan// nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor 'od 'phro ba// rgyab tu nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor ni// dpa' bo de yis bri bar bya// 'dri yi mdun du zi bya ba// dpa' bo mtha' yas pa yi
9a5(rgyud): zhal// stong phrag du ma'i phyag ldan ma// mtshan nyid thams cad yang dag rdzogs// rgyan rnams kun gyis rnam par brgyad// phyag gi rdo rje pad+ma 'chang // sna tshogs phyag rgyas phyag
9a6(rgyud): gzhan dkrigs// gtsug ldan dar gyi cod pan can// dbu rgyan pad+ma'i bzhin ras ma// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor dag la bzhugs// de 'odra nyi ma lta ba'i 'dra// dpa' bo'i rnal 'byor
9a7(rgyud): ldan pa yi// dpa' bo des ni bri bar bya// rdo rje sems dpar bdag bsgoms te// der ni snyems pas 'gro bar bya// dpa' bos lho ru bri bya ba// gshin rje'i 'dab ma mdzes pa la//
9b1(rgyud): mchog sbyin nam mkha' dge ma yang // rin chen khri la legs par bzhugs// bzhin ras sto la sngun dkar ba// 'dzum bcas nor bu'i 'og pag can// mgul rgyun rin chen 'phreng ba

9b5(rgyud): bar bya// de nas byang du phyin nas su// song ste dpa' bos bri bya ba// mi g.yo bzhin ras grags chen ma// mar gad 'bar ba mtshungs pa mo// dkar po'i dar gyis yang dag klubs//
9b6(rgyud): gtsug na nor bu cod pan bzang // gtsug rgyan sna tshogs dag gis spras// rdo rje dril bu'i lag bkra ma// sna tshogs rgyun dang gos ldan pas// zla ba'i gdun la yang dgra bzhugs//
9b7(rgyud): 'od kyis gtams pa'i dkyil 'khor mchog/ de nas mtshams kyi 'dab ma la// me tog bdug pa dri ldan ma// rdo rje snang byed dag pa ma'i// mchod pa sngags rig pa yis bris//
10a1(rgyud): gzugs sgra dri dang ro dang reg/ rang gi bdag po'i phyogs su'o// 'dab ma 'dab mar thams cad du// bzhad dang sgeg dang dbyangs chen mo// gar gyi phyag rgya
10a2(rgyud): grags chen po// sngags pas 'dab de bri bar bya// pad+ma la skyes 'dab ma la// thams cad du ni 'grub pa bri// sgo rnams dag ni thams cad la// sgo skyong ba ni rnam bzhi dang /

10a4(rgyud): tog 'phreng dang gos kyis brgyan// gtsug pud cod pan dang ldan zhing // mdzes pa'i dar gyis yang dag klubs// rdo rje dril bu lag par ldan// sbyor ba bzang ba'i rnam gzhag
10a5(rgyud): gis// de nas thams cad dgug par bya// rdo rje ma mo dka' thub che// bzlog dang rnal ma'i phyag rgya yis// rdo rje sems dpa' bzlas nas su// rdo rje'i sbyor bsu gar bya zhing /
10a6(rgyud): lan gsum du ni g.yas bskor bas// rdo rje ma mo'i dkyil 'khor rnams// dam tshig ldan pa thams cad byon// glu dbyangs kyi ni rgyal pos bskul// rang gi slob mo'i tshogs

10b2(rgyud): dradrug rang nyid kyi// rdzu 'phrul rnam par 'phrul pas byon// mtshan ma dag ni bzang po rnams// dkyil 'khor dag tu blta bar bya// rang ngam gzhan la bab sogs pa'i// mtshan ma
10b3(rgyud): ji ltar mthong ba na// de tshe nges par ma mo ni// bde gshegs thugs kyi dgongs par byon// de nas mchod yon zhabs bsil cho ga ji bzhin rab brtags te// de tshe babs pa'i sems

11a1(rgyud): dmyal bar 'dong bar 'gyur// des kyang yang dag de 'grub cing // myur du dmyal bar 'gro bar 'gyur// bgegs dang log par 'dren pa 'am// rims dang gdon
11a2(rgyud): dang dug sogs kyis// gdungs te nad kyis rgyun du ni// 'chi ba ru yang 'gyur ba yin// rdo rje slob dpon smad pa na// rtag tu dmyal ba nyid du ni// rab tu rmongs pa'i slob ma 'gro/ mkha'

11b1(rgyud): bum pa ru// dri yi chu yis yongs bkang la// dar dang ras sogs kyis g.yogs te// me tog rkun pos mgul brgyan nas// rin chen sman gyis rab bkang ba'i// gcig lhag bcu drug barba

12a1(rgyud): chen po rin chen bdun gyis bskor// lho yi phyogs su rin po che// nub tu pad+madz+ra nyid yin te// byang ngu ral gri rnon po'o// 'bar ba'i 'phreng 'khrugs 'od byeng cad/

12a7(rgyud): phul byas nas// slob dpon gyi ni zhabs la btud// ma dang chung ma bu mo dang // sring mo sring mo'i bu mo dang // bu rnams dang ni bdag nyid dang // rgyal po longs spyod gter dang ni/

23a7(rgyud): 'grub// nyi ma gsum gyi rgyal po mchog/ gdon mi za bar thob par 'gyur// bram ze'i bu mo skal chen mo// nor chen la ni bsgrub par bya// rje rigs sna tshogs sbyor ba yis//
23b1(rgyud): mtshungs pa nyid du bsgrub par bya// de yis dngos grub mchog rnyed de// rgyal po 'jig rten gsum gyi rjed// dmangs mo dpa' bo'i sbyor ba yis// bsgrubs na sngags kyi dngos grub 'gyur//
23b2(rgyud): gdod sbyin rgyal mchog grub pa dang // gnod sbyin rnams kyi dbang phyug mchog/ dman pa'i sems su bshad pa dang // mchog gis mchog ni chen po dang // bar mas bar ma'i dngos
23b3(rgyud): grub ni// skye ba 'di la thob par 'gyur// de nus las rnams bslab par bya// zhi ba dang ni rgyas pa'i las// de bzhin dbang dang mngon spyod dang // gzhan pa yi yang snga tshogs
23b4(rgyud): ni/ sems can rnams la dga' ba'o// shes rab pha rol phyin dge ma// dkyil 'khor sbyor bas bsgom par bya// kun da dkar po zla ba 'dra// 'od zer dkar pos mdzes pa
23b5(rgyud): mo// skye bo nad pa 'chi ka ma// de yi lus la gzhug par bya// de nas de ni stobs ldan 'gyur// brgyad gnyis pa yi lang tsher ldan// nad rnams kun lus rnam par grol// rga
23b6(rgyud): dang 'tsho ba rnam par spangs// bstan bcos kun gyi don rig cing // shes rab dran pa mchog dang ldan// de bzhin rang 'gyur rnal 'byor pa// nam mkha' la ni yang dag bsgom// mdzes

25a1(rgyud): pa'i me dang mtshungs pa mo// g.yon pa ru ni khro mo che// ma spyom ma ni ska rags mgul// las kyi rdo rje dri ldan mchog/ mche ba rnam par gtsigs pa'i zhal// gtsug na thod pa

80a6(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsal to// bcom ldan 'das bdag gis kyang rdo rje kung+gA nas 'bar shing me lce gcig tu gyur pa 'dis de'i rigs rgyud drang brgyas pa bsgrag

80b1(rgyud): na rdo rje la bka' stsal pa/ lag na rdo rje des lha mo sgrol ma'i phyag rgya bcings te spyan drangs la mdun du bzhag te/ de nas sngags pas b+ha gar zhugs te lus dang rtswa gcig tu byas/
80b2(rgyud): nas 'o ma'i mdog tu bsams te/ de las 'jig rten dbang phyug gi gzugs su bskyed do// yang lha mo sgrol ma sbyor ba 'dis 'jig rten dbang phyug gi ting nge 'dzin
80b3(rgyud): gyis bsten par bya'o// de nas lha mo dgyes nas mchog gsol bar 'gyur ro// de nas lha mo de rmi lam du 'ongs te 'khyud nas rgyan thams cad kyis brgyan cing yid du 'ong ba rol

81a1(rgyud): par bya'o// de nas gal te lag pa gnyis steng du bkrol na dge bar shes par bya'o// gal te 'og tu gnas na dge ba'ang ma yin/ mi dge ba'ang ma yin
81a2(rgyud): par shes par bya'o// gal te rgyab tu son par gyur na mi dge bar shes par bya'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das lha mo skul byed ma sgrub par 'dod na des de'i b+ha ga'i dbus su phyag na rdo rje'i

81a4(rgyud): de nas de'i kha dog gi dbye bas las byed de/ rgyas pa la kha dog ser po/ zhi ba la kha dog dkar po/ dbang la kha dog dmar po/ mngon spyod la kha dog nag po'o// 'di ltar
